meshObjects API

meshObjects represent the core data model of meshStack. The meshObject API is a REST API that allows you to get, create, update and delete meshObjects.

Depending on your use case you can consider the declarative import API as an alternative to the REST API.

Index

The root endpoint of the meshObject API provides links to all other meshObject endpoints in the API. You can use this endpoint to discover all available meshObject endpoints your authenticated user has access to.

Table 1. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshobjects.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshobjects.v2.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshobjects.v2.hal+json'
Table 2. Response Fields
Path Type Description

_links

Object

All available meshObject Links for the authenticated user.
Links

List of all meshObject endpoints the authenticated user has access to. Depending on your rights, you will only get a subset of the links mentioned here.

Relation Description

meshworkspaces

Get meshWorkspaces.

meshworkspaceusergroups

Get meshWorkspaceUserGroups.

meshprojects

Get meshProjects.

meshprojectgroupbindings

Gets meshProjectGroupBindings for this meshProject.

meshprojectuserbindings

Gets meshProjectUserBindings for this meshProject.

meshworkspaceuserbindings

Get meshWorkspaceUserBindings.

meshworkspacegroupbindings

Get meshWorkspaceGroupBindings.

meshprojectroles

Get meshProjectRoles.

meshtenants

Get meshTenants.

meshpaymentmethods

Get meshPaymentMethods.

meshplatforms

Get meshPlatforms.

meshusers

Get meshUsers.

meshserviceinstances

Get meshServiceInstances.

meshbuildingblocks

Get meshBuildingBlocks.

meshbuildingblockdefinitions

Get <meshBuildingBlockDefinitions.

meshbuildingblockruns

Get meshBuildingBlockRuns.

meshtagdefinitions

Get meshTagDefinitions.

meshcommunications

Get meshCommunications.

meshlandingzones

Get meshLandingZones.

meshBuildingBlock

All endpoints on meshBuildingBlocks.

List meshBuildingBlocks

Provides a paged list of meshBuildingBlocks.

Table 3. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 4. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

workspaceIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshWorkspace with given identifier. (optional)

projectIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshProject with given identifier. (optional)

platformIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshPlatform with given identifier. (optional)

name

Filter for Building Blocks with the given display name. (optional)

definitionName

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the definition with the given name. (optional)

definitionUuid

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the definition with the given uuid. (optional)

versionNumber

Filter for Building Blocks that use a certain version number. Can be the number or only 'v1', etc. (optional)

status

Filter for Building Blocks that have a certain status. One of WAITING_FOR_DEPENDENT_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_OPERATOR_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_USER_INPUT, PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED, FAILED, ABORTED. (optional)

page

The page number (default=0). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

size

The amount of elements in a single page (default=50). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks?projectIdentifier=my-project&page=0&size=10 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks?projectIdentifier=my-project&page=0&size=10' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json'
Table 5. Response Fields
Path Type Description

_embedded

Object

Contains the actual content of the paged response.

_embedded.meshBuildingBlocks[]

Array

List of meshBuildingBlocks.

page

Object

Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

_links

Object

Contains the self link, a link to the related tenant and pagination links.

X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 2947

Get meshBuildingBlock

Get a single meshBuildingBlock.

Table 6. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/5646eafe-5d56-43e5-84fe-329bb050d720 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/5646eafe-5d56-43e5-84fe-329bb050d720' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json'
Table 7. Response Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of Building Block datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshBuildingBlock' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'uuid' to uniquely identify the Building Block. It also contains additional meta information like the Building Block creation date.

metadata.uuid

String

The UUID to uniquely identify the Building Block.

metadata.definitionUuid

String

The UUID of the Building Block Definition this Building Block is based on.

metadata.definitionVersion

Number

The version number of the Building Block Definition this Building Block is based on.

metadata.tenantIdentifier

String

The full identifier of the tenant, this Building Block is created in.

metadata.forcePurge

Boolean

Set to true, if an operator explicitly requested this Building Block to be purged.

metadata.createdOn

String

The Building Block has been created at this date (e.g. 2020-12-22T09:37:43Z).

metadata.markedForDeletionOn

String

If the Building Block has been marked for deletion, the date when a user requested the deletion is provided via this field. e.g. 2020-12-22T09:37:43Z

metadata.markedForDeletionBy

String

If the Building Block has already been deleted, the username of the user who triggered the deletion is provided here.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the Building Block.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the Building Block as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.inputs[]

Array

List of inputs, which are set on the Building Block.

spec.inputs[].key

String

The key of the input as set on the related Building Block Definition.

spec.inputs[].value

String

The value, which is set on this input.

spec.inputs[].valueType

String

The data type of the value. One of STRING, CODE, INTEGER, BOOLEAN, FILE, LIST, SINGLE_SELECT, MULTI_SELECT.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[]

Array

List of parent building blocks, which are set on the Building Block.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].buildingBlockUuid

String

The UUID of the parent Building Block.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].definitionUuid

String

The UUID of the Building Block Definition of the parent Building Block.

status

Object

All fields in this section describe the current status of the Building Block.

status.status

String

The status of the Building Block. One of WAITING_FOR_DEPENDENT_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_OPERATOR_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_USER_INPUT, PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED, FAILED, ABORTED.

status.outputs[]

Array

List of outputs, which are set on the Building Block.

status.outputs[].key

String

The key of the output as set on the related Building Block Definition.

status.outputs[].value

String

The value, which is set on this output.

status.outputs[].valueType

String

The data type of the value. One of STRING, CODE, INTEGER, BOOLEAN, FILE, LIST, SINGLE_SELECT, MULTI_SELECT.

_links

Object

Available links on a Building Block.
Table 8. Building Block Links
Relation Description

meshtenant

Link to fetch the related meshTenant.

forcePurge

Link to purge this meshBuildingBlock. This is not available for workspace scoped access.

Post meshBuildingBlock

Create a new meshBuildingBlock.

Table 9. Request Headers
Name Description

Content-Type

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
POST /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v1.hal+json
Content-Length: 599
Host: mesh-backend-url

{
  "apiVersion" : "v1",
  "kind" : "meshBuildingBlock",
  "metadata" : {
    "definitionUuid" : "ef6aaf87-3f8c-477c-94f4-f3cf509728ca",
    "definitionVersion" : 1,
    "tenantIdentifier" : "my-workspace.my-project.my-platform.my-location"
  },
  "spec" : {
    "displayName" : "New BuildingBlock",
    "inputs" : [{
      "key": "resourceName",
      "value": "buildingBlock-for-docs",
      "valueType": "STRING"

    }]
  }
}

Table 10. Request Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of Building Block datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshBuildingBlock' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Fixed fields that help identify the Building Block.

metadata.definitionUuid

String

The UUID of the Building Block Definition this Building Block is based on.

metadata.definitionVersion

Number

The version number of the Building Block Definition this Building Block is based on.

metadata.tenantIdentifier

String

The full identifier of the tenant, this Building Block is created in.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the Building Block.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the Building Block as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.inputs[]

Array

List of inputs, which are set on the Building Block.

spec.inputs[].key

String

The key of the input as set on the related Building Block Definition.

spec.inputs[].value

String

The value, which is set on this input.

spec.inputs[].valueType

String

The data type of the value. One of STRING, CODE, INTEGER, BOOLEAN, FILE, LIST, SINGLE_SELECT, MULTI_SELECT.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[]

Array

List of parent building blocks, which are required for the Building Block. If none given, an empty list needs to be provided.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].buildingBlockUuid

String

The UUID of the parent Building Block.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].definitionUuid

String

The UUID of the Building Block Definition of the parent Building Block.

Relation Description

      "href" : "https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6"
    },
    "meshtenant" : {
      "href" : "https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshtenants/my-workspace.my-project.my-platform.my-location"
    },
    "forcePurge" : {
      "href" : "https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6/purge"
    }
  }
}
Delete meshBuildingBlock

Remove an existing meshBuildingBlock. Depending on the deletion mode of the meshBuildingBlock’s version, the meshBuildingBlock will either be removed (including potential cloud resources) or purged (removed from meshStack only).

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response
HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Purge meshBuildingBlock

With administration rights it is also possible to force the purging of a meshBuildingBlock. That way, the deletion mode of the meshBuildingBlock’s version is ignored and the meshBuildingBlock is deleted from meshStack.

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6/purge HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6/purge' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response
HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY

meshBuildingBlockRun (BETA)

Attention: This API is currently in BETA and subject to change.

Services which are called block runner are responsible for executing block runs. Those services use this API to execute and update the run status in meshStack. At the moment it is not possible to create and integrate a fully custom block runner, however you can use this API to send back status updates of individual block runs when you build an asynchronous building block (this is a building block which gets its execution handed over to an external system by the block runner). You need an API key with the permission to update building block runs. Please be aware that you can only update runs whose underlying building block definitions are owned by the workspace the API key is scoped to.

Register Sources and Steps

In order to return updates for a run to meshStack, you first need to register one or multiple steps and their resources of your run execution. It is up to you how many or how you organize your steps. You can however also just send step results back and the registration takes place on the fly, but in order to have a consistent display and ordering of steps, it is highly advised to pre-register steps and sources.

Table 12. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Request Body
{
  "source": {
    "id": "github",
    "externalRunId": "12345",
    "externalRunUrl": "https://github.com/meshcloud/example/actions/runs/12345678"
  },
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "displayName": "Init",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "displayName": "Pipeline"
  }]
}
Example Request
POST /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockruns/b3116611-e08b-4b00-91c5-10365b25a6ef/status/source HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json
Content-Length: 308
Host: mesh-backend-url

{
  "source": {
    "id": "github",
    "externalRunId": "12345",
    "externalRunUrl": "https://github.com/meshcloud/example/actions/runs/12345678"
  },
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "displayName": "Init",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "displayName": "Pipeline"
  }]
}
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockruns/b3116611-e08b-4b00-91c5-10365b25a6ef/status/source' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json' \
    -d '{
  "source": {
    "id": "github",
    "externalRunId": "12345",
    "externalRunUrl": "https://github.com/meshcloud/example/actions/runs/12345678"
  },
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "displayName": "Init",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "displayName": "Pipeline"
  }]
}  '
Table 13. Request Fields
Path Type Description

source.id

String

The ID of this source.

source.externalRunId

String

In case the external run is tracked by a different ID you can include it here

source.externalRunUrl

String

You can provide a clickable URL to a website with additional information about the external run.

steps[]

Array

Contains the steps for this source. It should not exceed more than 50 steps

steps[].id

String

The ID of this step.

steps[].displayName

String

The human readable display name of the step

steps[].status

String

The execution status of this step. Can be PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED or FAILED.
Update Sources and Steps

With this API you can update the step execution result. You can also provide the outputs of a building block run step, which will potentially be used as inputs of other dependent building blocks.

Table 14. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Request Body
{
  "status": "IN_PROGRESS",
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "status": "SUCCEEDED",
    "userMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "systemMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "outputs": {
      "outputName": {
        "value": "hello-world",
        "type": "STRING",
        "isSensitive": false
      }
    }
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  }]
}
Example Request
PATCH /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockruns/b3116611-e08b-4b00-91c5-10365b25a6ef/status/source/github HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json
Content-Length: 381
Host: mesh-backend-url

{
  "status": "IN_PROGRESS",
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "status": "SUCCEEDED",
    "userMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "systemMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "outputs": {
      "outputName": {
        "value": "hello-world",
        "type": "STRING",
        "isSensitive": false
      }
    }
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  }]
}
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockruns/b3116611-e08b-4b00-91c5-10365b25a6ef/status/source/github' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X PATCH \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockrun.v1.hal+json' \
    -d '{
  "status": "IN_PROGRESS",
  "steps": [{
    "id": "step1",
    "status": "SUCCEEDED",
    "userMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "systemMessage": "Step was successful.",
    "outputs": {
      "outputName": {
        "value": "hello-world",
        "type": "STRING",
        "isSensitive": false
      }
    }
  },
  {
    "id": "step2",
    "status": "IN_PROGRESS"
  }]
}  '
Table 15. Request Fields
Path Type Description

status

String

The execution status of the building block as whole. Can be any of PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED, ABORTED or FAILED. (Optional)

steps[]

Array

Can contain updates to the steps. (Optional)

steps[].id

String

The ID of the step which should get updates.

steps[].userMessage

String

A message which is displayed to the user. It should not exceed more than 500 characters. (Optional)

steps[].systemMessage

String

A message which is displayed only to the operators. It should not exceed more than 500 characters. (Optional)

steps[].outputs

Object

Contains any output this step has provided. (Optional)

steps[].outputs.outputName.value

Varies

The name of the input variable.

steps[].outputs.outputName.type

Varies

The type of the variable. It can be one of mesh_buildingblockrun_iotype

steps[].outputs.outputName.isSensitive

Varies

Flag if the variable content is sensitive and encrypted. The runner must decrypt this variable content first before it can be used. Information on how to do this will provided in the future.

steps[].status

String

The execution status of this step. Can be PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED, ABORTED or FAILED. (Optional)
Usable Output Types

  • STRING: A simple text output.

  • INTEGER: A numeric output.

  • BOOLEAN: A boolean flag

Pragma: no-cache

  "runAborted" : false

  "status": "ABORTED"
}

meshBuildingBlock (v2-preview)

All endpoints on meshBuildingBlocks (v2-preview).

List meshBuildingBlocks

Provides a paged list of meshBuildingBlocks (v2-preview).

Table 16. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblock.v2-preview.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 17. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

workspaceIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshWorkspace with given identifier. These are all Building Blocks that either belong directly to the meshWorkspace or to any meshTenant of one of the its meshProjects. (optional)

projectIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshProject with given identifier. The result will only contain Building Blocks on tenant level. (optional)

platformIdentifier

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshPlatform with given identifier. The result will only contain Building Blocks on tenant level. (optional)

name

Filter for Building Blocks with the given display name. (optional)

definitionUuid

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the definition with the given uuid. (optional)

versionUuid

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the definition version with the given uuid. (optional)

tenantUuid

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to the meshTenant with the given uuid. (optional)

targetRefKind

Filter for Building Blocks that belong to a target of given kind. Must be either 'meshTenant' or 'meshWorkspace'. (optional)

status

Filter for Building Blocks that have a certain status. One of WAITING_FOR_DEPENDENT_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_OPERATOR_INPUT, WAITING_FOR_USER_INPUT, PENDING, IN_PROGRESS, SUCCEEDED, FAILED, ABORTED. (optional)

managedByWorkspaceIdentifier

Lists Building Blocks that are managed by the workspace with given identifier. Requires API key permission 'List all Building Blocks for owned definition'. Takes precedence over the 'managedByDefinitionUuid' parameter. (optional)

managedByDefinitionUuid

Lists Building Blocks that are created based on the definition with given uuid. Requires API key permission 'List all Building Blocks for owned definition'. (optional)

page

The page number (default=0). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

size

The amount of elements in a single page (default=50). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

Path Type Description

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshBuildingBlock' for this endpoint.

Object

All fields in this section describe the Building Block.

Object

The reference to the meshBuildingBlockDefinitionVersion for this Building Block

String

Object

The reference to either a tenant or workspace the Building Block is located on.

String

String

String

String

String

The value, which is set on this input.

spec.inputs[].valueType

String

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[]

Array

List of parent Building Blocks, which are required for the Building Block. If none given, an empty list needs to be provided.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].buildingBlockUuid

String

The UUID of the parent Building Block.

spec.parentBuildingBlocks[].definitionUuid

String

The UUID of the Building Block Definition of the parent Building Block.

Delete meshBuildingBlock

Remove an existing meshBuildingBlock. Depending on the deletion mode of the meshBuildingBlock’s version, the meshBuildingBlock will either be removed (including potential cloud resources) or purged (removed from meshStack only).

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response
HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Purge meshBuildingBlock

With administration rights it is also possible to force the purging of a meshBuildingBlock. That way, the deletion mode of the meshBuildingBlock’s version is ignored and the meshBuildingBlock is deleted from meshStack.

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6/purge HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblocks/188922e3-7c9a-471d-bbd7-73e88bd05fa6/purge' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response
HTTP/1.1 202 Accepted
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY
meshBuildingBlock targetRef

A target reference is a reference to either the tenant or the workspace the Building Block is located on. It looks like one of the examples below:

{
  "kind": "meshWorkspace",
  "identifier": "workspaceIdentifier"
}
{
  "kind": "meshTenant",
  "uuid": "uuid-of-the-tenant"
}

Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of Building Block Definition datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshBuildingBlockDefinition' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'uuid' to uniquely identify the Building Block Definition. It also contains additional meta information like the Building Block Definition creation date.

metadata.uuid

String

The UUID to uniquely identify the Building Block Definition.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

The identifier of the meshWorkspace the Building Blocks Definition belongs to.

metadata.createdOn

String

The Building Block Definition has been created at this date (e.g. 2020-12-22T09:37:43Z).

metadata.tags

Object

Key/Value pairs of tags set on the Building Block Definition. Keep in mind, that values are an array.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the Building Block Definition.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.description

String

The description of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.supportUrl

String

The URL pointing to support of the Building Block Definition. (optional)

spec.documentationUrl

String

The URL pointing to documentation of the Building Block Definition. (optional)

spec.supportedPlatforms

Array

List of the platforms this Building Block Definition supports

spec.runTransparency

Boolean

Specifies the Building Block Definition run control. When set to true, both platform teams and workspace users can view detailed run logs and re-run building blocks. When set to false (default), only platform teams have this access.

spec.useInLandingZonesOnly

Boolean

Indicated whether this Building Block Definitions should be used on Landing Zones only.

spec.notificationSubscriberUsernames

Array

A list of usernames from the users that should be notified as subscribers for this Building Block Definition.

spec.symbol

String

The symbol of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.targetType

String

The type of Building Block Definition. (One of [TENANT_LEVEL, WORKSPACE_LEVEL])

status

Object

All fields in this section describe the current status of the Building Block Definition.

status.versions[]

Array

List of meshBuildingBlockDefinitionVersions, which exist for the Building Block Definition.

status.latestVersion

Number

The number of the latest version based on this Building Block Definition including a possible draft version.

status.latestReleasedVersion

Number

The number of the latest version based on this Building Block Definition not including a possible draft version.

status.versions[].versionNumber

Number

The number of the listed version.

status.versions[].versionUuid

String

The uuid of the listed version

status.versions[].state

String

The state of the listed version. (One of [DRAFT, RELEASED])

Object

Available links on a Building Block Definition.

$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockdefinitions/27b51b8e-0470-423b-b936-24d40133e04c' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X PUT \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockdefinition.v1-preview.hal+json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshbuildingblockdefinition.v1-preview.hal+json' \
    -d '{
  "apiVersion" : "v1-preview",
  "kind" : "meshBuildingBlockDefinition",
  "metadata" : {
    "uuid": "27b51b8e-0470-423b-b936-24d40133e04c",
    "ownedByWorkspace": "my-workspace"
  },
  "spec" : {
    "targetType": "TENANT_LEVEL",
    "displayName": "BB definition example",
    "description": "description - updated",
    "supportUrl": "https://example.com",
    "documentationUrl": "https://example.com",
    "supportedPlatforms" : [ "AZURE" ],
    "useInLandingZonesOnly": false,
    "runTransparency": false,
    "notificationSubscriberUsernames": []
  }
}'
Table 35. Request Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of Building Block Definition datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshBuildingBlockDefinition' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'uuid' to uniquely identify the Building Block Definition. It also contains additional meta information like the Building Block Definition creation date.

metadata.uuid

String

The uuid of the Building Blocks Definition.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

The identifier of the meshWorkspace the Building Blocks Definition belongs to.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the Building Block Definition.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.description

String

The description of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.supportUrl

String

The URL pointing to support of the Building Block Definition. (optional)

spec.documentationUrl

String

The URL pointing to documentation of the Building Block Definition. (optional)

spec.supportedPlatforms

Array

List of the platforms this Building Block Definition supports

spec.runTransparency

Boolean

Specifies the Building Block Definition run control. When set to true, both platform teams and workspace users can view detailed run logs and re-run building blocks. When set to false (default), only platform teams have this access. (Optional)

spec.useInLandingZonesOnly

Boolean

Indicated whether this Building Block Definitions should be used on Landing Zones only.

spec.notificationSubscriberUsernames

Array

A list of usernames from the users that should be notified as subscribers for this Building Block Definition.

spec.symbol

String

The symbol of the Building Block Definition as it is shown in meshPanel. (optional)

spec.targetType

String

The type of Building Block Definition. (One of [TENANT_LEVEL, WORKSPACE_LEVEL])
Table 36. Building Block Definition Links
Relation Description

owner

Link to fetch the owning meshWorkspace.

buildingblocks

Link to fetch meshBuildingBlocks that belong to this Building Block Definition.

Delete meshBuildingBlockDefinition

Remove an existing meshBuildingBlockDefinition and all its versions.

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockdefinitions/27b51b8e-0470-423b-b936-24d40133e04c HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshbuildingblockdefinitions/27b51b8e-0470-423b-b936-24d40133e04c' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE

meshCommunication (preview)

All endpoints on meshCommunications.

the meshCommunication endpoint is still in preview mode, which means it is subject to change and we are planning to introduce a new version without support for backwards compatibility, meaning, the preview version will disappear without prior warning! If this is not acceptable, please wait until the final meshCommunication endpoints are announced in the release notes. These endpoints will be released in the next few weeks. From then on, we will provide backwards-compatible communication endpoints, meaning, once new versions are introduced, you can continue to use older versions by setting the correct Accept header.

The meshCommunication endpoints are only available if the developer engagement module is activated in your meshStack. If you would like to enable this feature, please contact us at support@meshcloud.io

List meshCommunications

Provides a paged list of meshCommunications.

Table 37. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

meshApi is versioned and you should use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json as an Accept header to be guaranteed the V1 response format of this endpoint. New versions will be added in future.
Table 38. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

communicationDefinitionUuid

Filter for communications that belong to the definition with the given uuid. (optional)

resolutionStatus

Filter for communications with the given resolution status (OPEN, RESOLVED). (optional)

communicationType

Filter for communications where the associated definition has the given communication type (ACTION_REQUIRED, NOTIFICATION). (optional)

page

The page number (default=0). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

size

The amount of elements in a single page (default=50). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshcommunications?communicationDefinitionUuid=449aa758-3a46-42bd-9645-dd424e45abea&resolutionStatus=OPEN&communicationType=ACTION_REQUIRED&page=0&size=3 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshcommunications?communicationDefinitionUuid=449aa758-3a46-42bd-9645-dd424e45abea&resolutionStatus=OPEN&communicationType=ACTION_REQUIRED&page=0&size=3' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json'
Table 39. Response Fields
Path Type Description

_embedded

Object

Contains the actual content of the paged response.

_embedded.meshCommunications[]

Array

List of meshCommunications.

page

Object

Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

_links

Object

Currently only contains the self link and pagination links.

Table 40. Request Headers
Name Description

GET /api/meshobjects/meshcommunications/013a18c8-3ce1-4bf4-9e08-c67555152d73 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=

Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshcommunications/013a18c8-3ce1-4bf4-9e08-c67555152d73' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json'
Table 41. Response Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of meshCommunication datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshCommunication' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'uuid' to uniquely identify the communication. It also contains additional meta information.

metadata.uuid

String

The UUID to uniquely identify the communication.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

The identifier of the workspace that owns the communication

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the communication.

spec.targetMeshObjectRef

Object

Describes the meshObject that is targeted by this communication

spec.targetMeshObjectRef.kind

String

What kind of meshObject is targeted (e.g. meshWorkspace)

spec.targetMeshObjectRef.name

String

An name or identifier to uniquely identify the targeted meshObject

spec.communicationDefinitionRef

Object

Reference to the associated communication definition.

spec.communicationDefinitionRef.uuid

String

UUID of the associated communication definition.

spec.communicationDefinitionRef.kind

String

This is a fixed value "meshCommunicationDefinition"

status

Object

contains the current status as well as the associated meshCommunicationDefinition

status.resolutionStatus

String

only present if the associated communication definition is of type ACTION_REQUIRED. Either OPEN or RESOLVED.

status.meshCommunicationDefinition

Object

the communication definition associated to this communication.

status.meshCommunicationDefinition.uuid

String

The UUID that uniquely identifies the meshCommunicationDefinition.

status.meshCommunicationDefinition.title

String

The title of the meshCommunicationDefinition.

status.meshCommunicationDefinition.communicationType

String

Either NOTIFICATION or ACTION_REQUIRED.

status.meshCommunicationDefinition.dueDate

String

The due date of the meshCommunicationDefinition in ISO 8601 format (YYYY-MM-DD). Only present if a due date was specified for the communication definition.

_links

Object

Currently only contains the self link.

Post meshCommunication

Create a new meshCommunication. A meshCommunication is attached to a meshCommunicationDefinition, therefore, a meshCommunicationDefinition must exist before you can create a meshCommunication.

Table 42. Request Headers
Name Description

Content-Type

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
POST /api/meshobjects/meshcommunications HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunication.v1-preview.hal+json
Content-Length: 327
Host: mesh-backend-url

{

Table 43. Request Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of Communication datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshCommunication' for this endpoint.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the Communication.

spec.targetMeshObjectRef

Object

describes which meshObject is targeted.

spec.targetMeshObjectRef.kind

String

The type of mesh object being targeted. Supported values are: meshWorkspace, meshTenant, and meshBuildingBlock.

spec.targetMeshObjectRef.name

String

An identifier or UUID that uniquely identifies the referenced meshObject. The required format depends on the kind of the target: For kind meshWorkspace, use the workspace identifier. For kind meshTenant, use the tenant UUID. For kind meshBuildingBlock, use the building block UUID.

spec.communicationDefinitionRef

Object

Reference to the associated communication definition.

spec.communicationDefinitionRef.uuid

String

The UUID of the communication definition associated with this communication.

spec.communicationDefinitionRef.kind

String

This is a fixed value "meshCommunicationDefinition"

meshCommunicationDefinition (preview)

All endpoints on meshCommunicationDefinitions.

the meshCommunicationDefinition endpoint is still in preview mode, which means it is subject to change and we are planning to introduce a new version without support for backwards compatibility, meaning, the preview version will disappear without prior warning! If this is not acceptable, please wait until the final meshCommunicationDefinition endpoints are announced in the release notes. These endpoints will be released in the next few weeks. From then on, we will provide backwards-compatible communication definition endpoints, meaning, once new versions are introduced, you can continue to use older versions by setting the correct Accept header.

The meshCommunicationDefinition endpoints are only available if the developer engagement module is activated in your meshStack. If you would like to enable this feature, please contact us at support@meshcloud.io

Post meshCommunicationDefinition

Create a new meshCommunicationDefinition. A meshCommunicationDefinition defines a group of meshCommunications with a common purpose and target audience. Each definition includes a communication message and metadata like due date. Notice that separate API calls to the meshCommunication API have to be made in order for recipients to receive the message. Therefore, you’ll usually want to fetch the metadata.uuid returned by this API call and subsequently put that UUID into the metadata.definitionUuid field when creating a communication via the meshCommunication API endpoint.

Table 49. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunicationdefinition.v1-preview.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Content-Type

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshcommunicationdefinition.v1-preview.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Path Type Description

kind

Kind of mesh object, always 'meshCommunicationDefinition'.

Title of the communication.

spec.communication.message

String

Content of the message.

spec.communication.type

String

Type of communication: ACTION_REQUIRED or NOTIFICATION.

spec.communication.dueDate

String

Due date in ISO 8601 format.

Response Fields

The fields have the same meaning as the request fields, with the exception of the following fields, which are absent from the request fields:

Path Type Description

status.communicationsTotal

Number

the total amount of communications associated to this definition.

status.communicationsResolved

Number

the amount of resolved communications. This field is only present for communication definitions of type ACTION_REQUIRED, because other types of communications are not meant to be resolved.

status.communicationsOpen

Number

the amount of open (unresolved) communications. This field is only present for communication definitions of type ACTION_REQUIRED, because other types of communications are not meant to be resolved.

The amount of communications shown in the response will be 0 after a communication definition was created. You have to explicitly create new meshCommunications via separate API requests on the meshCommunication endpoint.

Platform Properties

The following convention is used for the spec.platformProperties object:

{
  "platformProperties" : {
    "type": "$PLATFORM",
    "$PLATFORM": { … all platform specific properties … }
  }
}

For example, in the case of AWS:

{
  "platformProperties" : {
    "type": "aws",
    "aws": { … all AWS specific properties … }
  }
}

or GCP:

{
  "platformProperties" : {
    "type": "gcp",
    "gcp": { … all GCP specific properties … }
  }
}

The following tables list all required and optional properties for the supported platform types.

GCP
Table 62. Request Fields
Path Type Description

spec.platformProperties.type

String

The platform type, gcp in this case.

spec.platformProperties.gcp.gcpCloudFunctionUrl

String

Optional. If a GCP Cloud Function URL is provided it is getting called at the end of the replication process.

spec.platformProperties.gcp.gcpFolderId

String

Google Cloud Projects will be added to this Google Cloud Folder. This allows applying Organization Policies to all projects managed under this Landing Zone.

spec.platformProperties.gcp.gcpTemplateUrl

String

Optional. URL to a GCP bucket (starts with 'gs://') with a template config. The template is deployed in the project during the replication process. Only YAML files are supported with a file size limit of 1 MB.

spec.platformProperties.gcp.gcpRoleMappings

Array

You can use both built-in roles like 'roles/editor' or custom roles like 'organizations/123123123123/roles/meshstack.project_developer'. For more information see the Landing Zone documentation. Multiple GCP Roles can be assigned to one meshRole. If empty, the default that is configured on platform level will be used.
Example Request
POST /api/meshobjects/meshlandingzones HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshlandingzone.v1-preview.hal+json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshlandingzone.v1-preview.hal+json
Content-Length: 1351
Host: mesh-backend-url

{
  "apiVersion" : "v1-preview",
  "kind" : "meshLandingZone",
  "metadata" : {
    "name" : "new-landing-zone-gcp",
    "tags" : { }
  },
  "spec" : {
    "displayName" : "New Landing Zone gcp",
    "description" : "A new gcp landing zone for testing",
    "platformRef" : {
      "uuid" : "943e605b-160b-421d-9992-6bfc1b5f81b0",
      "kind" : "meshPlatform"
    },
    "automateDeletionApproval" : false,
    "automateDeletionReplication" : false,
    "infoLink" : "https://example.com/info",
    "platformProperties" : {
      "type" : "gcp",
      "gcp" : {
        "gcpFolderId" : "12345",
        "gcpTemplateUrl" : "gs://my-bucket-name/folder/template",
        "gcpCloudFunctionUrl" : "https://us-central1-my-sample-project.cloudfunctions.net/helloWorld",
        "gcpRoleMappings" : [ {
          "projectRoleRef" : {
            "name" : "owner",
            "kind" : "meshProjectRole"
          },
          "platformRoles" : [ "roles/owner" ]
        }, {
          "projectRoleRef" : {
            "name" : "editor",
            "kind" : "meshProjectRole"
          },
          "platformRoles" : [ "roles/editor" ]
        }, {
          "projectRoleRef" : {
            "name" : "reader",
            "kind" : "meshProjectRole"
          },
          "platformRoles" : [ "roles/editor", "roles/viewer" ]
        } ]
      }
    }
  }
}
AWS
Table 63. Request Fields
Path Type Description

spec.platformProperties.type

String

The platform type, aws in this case.

spec.platformProperties.aws.awsTargetOrgUnitId

String

The created AWS account for this Landing Zone will be put under the given Organizational Unit. You can also input a Root ID (starting with 'r-') then the account will be put directly under this root without assigning it to an OU (this is not recommended).

spec.platformProperties.aws.awsEnrollAccount

Boolean

If true, accounts will be enrolled to AWS control tower. In case an enrollment configuration is provided for the AWS platform AND this value is set to true, created AWS accounts will automatically be enrolled with AWS Control Tower. Automatic account enrollment does also require the Target Organizational Unit to already be enrolled with AWS Control Tower and the corresponding meshfed-service role needs to be in the "IAM Principal" list for the Portfolio access of the Account Factory Product ID you defined in platform settings. Click here to learn more about the Control Tower setup.

spec.platformProperties.aws.awsLambdaArn

String

Optional. If this Lambda ARN is given, it is invoked after each project replication. You can use it to trigger a custom Account Vending Machine to perform several additional provisioning steps.

spec.platformProperties.aws.awsRoleMappings

Array

Roles can be mapped from the meshRole to the AWS Role. The AWS role will be part of the role or group name within AWS. If empty, the default that is configured on platform level will be used.

Content-Length: 1040
Host: mesh-backend-url

Azure
Table 64. Request Fields
Path Type Description

spec.platformProperties.type

String

The platform type, azure in this case.

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureRoleMappings

Array

An array of mappings between the meshRole and the Azure specific access role. If empty, default role mappings defined on meshPlatform level are used. For more information see the Landing Zone documentation. If empty, the default that is configured on platform level will be used.

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureRoleMappings[].azureGroupSuffix

String

The given role name will be injected into the group name via the group naming pattern configured on the platform instance.

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureRoleMappings[].azureRoleDefinitions

Array

Role Definitions with the given IDs will be attached to this Azure Role

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureRoleMappings[].azureRoleDefinitions[].abacCondition

String

Optional. an ABAC condition for the role assignment in form of a string

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureManagementGroupId

String

Subscriptions with this Landing Zone will be added to this Management Group. Please make sure to use the Management Group ID and not the group name!

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureFunction

Object

Optional. Assign an Azure function to the Landing Zone configuration to trigger a small piece of code in the cloud.

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureFunction.azureFunctionUrl

String

The URL of your Azure Function. This is typically a value like https://my-function-app.azurewebsites.net/myfunc

spec.platformProperties.azure.azureFunction.azureFunctionScope

String

Optional. the unique ID of the Azure Enterprise Application your function belongs to. More details are described here.

meshPaymentMethod

All endpoints on meshPaymentMethods.

List meshPaymentMethods

Provides a paged list of meshPaymentMethods. Deleted meshPaymentMethods are not provided via this endpoint.

Table 69. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshpaymentmethod.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 70. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

workspaceIdentifier

Filter for meshPaymentMethods that belong to the meshWorkspace with given identifier (optional). Note: the server will ignore this filter when the request principal does not have permission to read payment methods in any workspace.

page

The page number (default=0). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

size

The amount of elements in a single page (default=50). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshpaymentmethods?workspaceIdentifier=payment-workspace&page=0&size=2 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshpaymentmethod.v2.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshpaymentmethods?workspaceIdentifier=payment-workspace&page=0&size=2' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshpaymentmethod.v2.hal+json'
Table 71. Response Fields
Path Type Description

_embedded

Object

Contains the actual content of the paged response.

_embedded.meshPaymentMethods[]

Array

List of meshPaymentMethods.

_links

Object

Currently only contains the self link and pagination links.

page

Object

Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

Get meshPaymentMethod

Get a single meshPaymentMethod. Deleted meshPaymentMethods can also be requested via this endpoint. A future version of the meshPaymentMethod object will include additional fields to indicate the deletion state of a payment method.

Table 72. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshpaymentmethod.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshpaymentmethods/test-payment-method-1 HTTP/1.1

Table 73. Response Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of meshPaymentMethod datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshPaymentMethod' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'name' and (optional) 'ownedByWorkspace' to uniquely identify the meshPaymentMethod.

metadata.name

String

The paymentMethodIdentifier as 'name'.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

The workspaceIdentifier as 'ownedByWorkspace'.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the meshPaymentMethod.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the meshPaymentMethod as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.tags

Object

Key/Value pairs of tags set on the meshPaymentMethod. Keep in mind, that values are an array.

spec.amount

Number

The amount of the meshPaymentMethod.

spec.expirationDate

String

The expiration date (yyyy-MM-dd) of the meshPaymentMethod. The date is considered as UTC.

_links

Object

Available links on a meshPaymentMethod.
Table 74. PaymentMethod Links
Relation Description

meshprojects

Get meshProjects, that are assigned to this payment method. Substitute Payment Methods on meshProjects are not considered!

Update meshPaymentMethod

Update an existing meshPaymentMethod by identifier. This endpoint supports both updating an existing payment method as well as creating a new payment method if a payment method with this identifier does not exist yet.

Table 76. Request Headers
Name Description

Content-Type

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshpaymentmethod.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Accept

Delete meshPaymentMethod

Delete a meshPaymentMethod by identifier. meshStack currently only allows soft deletion of payment methods.

Please note that it’s possible to retrieve a payment method via the GET meshPaymentMethod endpoint after deletion.

meshPlatform

All endpoints on meshPlatforms.

A meshPlatform represents a cloud platform integration in meshStack. It defines how meshStack connects to and manages resources on cloud platforms like Azure, AWS, GCP, or Kubernetes clusters. Each meshPlatform is owned by a workspace and can be configured with specific access restrictions and marketplace availability.

Note: This API enables management for platform configuration around replication, but not yet for metering.

Note: This API does not yet support pricing on platforms.

Please refer to the meshPlatform Configurations section for details on how to configure meshPlatforms.

List meshPlatforms

Provides a paged list of meshPlatforms. Deleted meshPlatforms are not provided via this endpoint.

Depending on your permissions, you will see:

  • Admin users: All meshPlatforms in the system

  • Workspace users: Only meshPlatforms owned by their workspace, public platforms, or platforms they contribute to

Get meshPlatform

Get a single meshPlatform by its UUID. Deleted meshPlatforms are not provided via this endpoint. Please note that the configuration value is only filled for supported platform types. If the platform type is not supported, the configuration value will be empty. The supported platform types are listed here: meshPlatform Configurations.

Access is granted based on:

  • Platform ownership (workspace owns the platform)

  • Platform visibility (public platforms)

  • Platform contribution (workspace is a contributor)

  • Platform marketplace publication status

  • Admin permissions

Put meshPlatform

Update an existing meshPlatform by its UUID.

Warning

Please note that changing certain attributes like platform configuration can have serious consequences for existing tenants and ongoing operations. Changes to platform connectivity may disrupt:

  • Tenant replication processes

  • Metering data collection

  • User access to platform tenants

  • Building block operations

Proceed with caution and ensure proper testing in non-production environments.

Response Fields

A meshPlatform object. See meshPlatform Response Fields.

Delete meshPlatform

Delete a meshPlatform by its UUID.

Warning

Deleting a meshPlatform has significant consequences:

  • Tenants: All associated meshTenants will be automatically deleted in meshStack, but the actual cloud resources remain untouched

  • Billing: Usage reports for the current month won’t be finalized and won’t be included in chargeback statements

  • Access: Users lose access to platform tenants via meshStack (but can still access them directly in the cloud platform)

  • Identifier: You cannot create a new meshPlatform with the same identifier in the same location

This operation cannot be undone. Ensure you have proper backups and have communicated the impact to affected users.
Request Headers

meshPlatform Configurations

A meshPlatform has a specific type and based on that type needs to be configured with individual configuration fields. You find example configurations with explanation annotations in this section.

With the current version of this API the following meshPlatform types are supported:

  • Azure Kubernetes Service (AKS)

  • Amazon Web Services (AWS)

  • Microsoft Azure (Azure)

  • Azure Resource Group (AzureRG)

  • Google Cloud Platform (GCP)

  • Kubernetes clusters (Kubernetes)

  • OpenShift clusters (OpenShift)

The example configuration provided here belongs to the specification of the respective meshPlatform object like so:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "$PLATFORM",
        "$PLATFORM": { … all platform specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

For example, in the case of AWS:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "aws",
        "aws": { … all AWS specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

Or GCP:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "gcp",
        "gcp": { … all GCP specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

The following platform types are supported (i.e., spec.config.type must be one of the following values):

  • aks: Configuration for Azure Kubernetes Service

  • aws: Configuration for Amazon Web Services

  • azure: Configuration for Microsoft Azure

  • azurerg: Configuration for Azure Resource Group

  • gcp: Configuration for Google Cloud Platform

  • kubernetes: Configuration for Kubernetes clusters

  • openshift: Configuration for OpenShift clusters

Note: Currently, the meshPlatform API supports only the configuration needed for replication. Metering configuration is not yet supported. Existing metering configuration won’t be removed when a meshPlatform is updated.

All endpoints on meshPlatforms (v2-preview).

A meshPlatform represents a cloud platform integration in meshStack. It defines how meshStack connects to and manages resources on cloud platforms like Azure, AWS, GCP, or Kubernetes clusters. Each meshPlatform is owned by a workspace and can be configured with specific access restrictions and marketplace availability.

Note: This API enables management for platform configuration around replication, but not yet for metering.

Please refer to the meshPlatform Configurations (v2-preview) section for details on how to configure meshPlatforms.

  • Workspace users: Only meshPlatforms owned by their workspace, public platforms, or platforms they contribute to

Path Type Description

String

metadata

Object

Contains metadata to uniquely identify the meshPlatform.

metadata.name

String

The platform identifier as 'name' to identify the meshPlatform.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

String

String

Object

String

spec.description

String

spec.endpoint

String

Optional. The web console URL endpoint of the platform.

spec.supportUrl

String

Optional. URL for platform support documentation.

spec.documentationUrl

String

Optional. URL for platform documentation.

spec.locationRef

Object

Reference to the location where this platform is situated.

spec.locationRef.name

String

The identifier of the location.

spec.availability

Object

Availability configuration for the meshPlatform.

spec.availability.restriction

String

Access restriction level: PUBLIC, PRIVATE, or RESTRICTED.

spec.availability.restrictedToWorkspaces

Array

Optional. If the restriction is set to RESTRICTED, you can specify the workspace identifiers this meshPlatform is restricted to.

Array

Put meshPlatform

Update an existing meshPlatform by its UUID.

Warning

Please note that changing certain attributes like platform configuration can have serious consequences for existing tenants and ongoing operations. Changes to platform connectivity may disrupt:

  • Tenant replication processes

  • Metering data collection

  • User access to platform tenants

  • Building block operations

Proceed with caution and ensure proper testing in non-production environments.

Delete meshPlatform

Delete a meshPlatform by its UUID.

Warning

Deleting a meshPlatform has significant consequences:

  • Tenants: All associated meshTenants will be automatically deleted in meshStack, but the actual cloud resources remain untouched

  • Billing: Usage reports for the current month won’t be finalized and won’t be included in chargeback statements

  • Access: Users lose access to platform tenants via meshStack (but can still access them directly in the cloud platform)

  • Identifier: You cannot create a new meshPlatform with the same identifier in the same location

This operation cannot be undone. Ensure you have proper backups and have communicated the impact to affected users.
Request Headers

Unresolved directive in mesh_platform_v2.adoc - include::/__w/meshfed-release/meshfed-release/meshfed/api/build/generated-snippets/meshPlatformV2Delete/request-headers.adoc[]

meshPlatform Configurations (v2-preview)

A meshPlatform has a specific type and based on that type needs to be configured with individual configuration fields. You find example configurations with explanation annotations in this section.

With the current version of this API the following meshPlatform types are supported:

  • Azure Kubernetes Service (AKS)

  • Amazon Web Services (AWS)

  • Microsoft Azure (Azure)

  • Azure Resource Group (AzureRG)

  • Google Cloud Platform (GCP)

  • Kubernetes clusters (Kubernetes)

  • OpenShift clusters (OpenShift)

The example configuration provided here belongs to the specification of the respective meshPlatform object like so:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "$PLATFORM",
        "$PLATFORM": { … all platform specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

For example, in the case of AWS:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "aws",
        "aws": { … all AWS specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

Or GCP:

{
  "meshPlatform": {
    "metadata": { ... },
    "spec": {
      "displayName": "Example Platform",
      ...,
      "config": {
        "type": "gcp",
        "gcp": { … all GCP specific properties … }
      }
    },
    "status": { ... }
  }
}

The following platform types are supported (i.e., spec.config.type must be one of the following values):

  • aks: Configuration for Azure Kubernetes Service

  • aws: Configuration for Amazon Web Services

  • azure: Configuration for Microsoft Azure

  • azurerg: Configuration for Azure Resource Group

  • gcp: Configuration for Google Cloud Platform

  • kubernetes: Configuration for Kubernetes clusters

  • openshift: Configuration for OpenShift clusters

Note: Currently, the meshPlatform API supports only the configuration needed for replication. Metering configuration is not yet supported. Existing metering configuration won’t be removed when a meshPlatform is updated.

meshProject

All endpoints on meshProjects.

List meshProjects

Provides a paged list of meshProjects. By default only active projects are returned, but you can also explicitly filter for deleted and pending deletion projects.

Table 84. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 85. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

workspaceIdentifier

Filter for meshProjects that belong to the meshWorkspace with given identifier. (optional)

paymentIdentifier

Filter for meshProjects that have the meshPaymentMethod with given identifier assigned. Substitute Payment Methods on meshProjects are not considered! Use an empty or blank value to filter for meshProjects without an assigned meshPaymentMethod. (optional)

state

Filter for meshProjects with a certain deletion state. Possible values are:
[ACTIVE] (default option) All meshProjects that are not deleted or submitted for deletion,
[PENDING_DELETION] meshProjects which are in a state of deletion. It means the system is waiting for all tenants to be successfully deleted after all tenants are gone the project itself is deleted,
[DELETED] meshProjects which are fully deleted now, keep in mind that the identifier is changed (a timestamp is appended) after deletion so you might not use this as an identifying property.
You can search for different states at once when you separate them via a comma. This parameter is only usable from meshProject media type version 2 or higher.

page

The page number (default=0). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)

size

The amount of elements in a single page (default=50). Information about [paging](/api/technical-specifications/#paging)
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshprojects?workspaceIdentifier=bhlm7mpdsv2&paymentIdentifier=test-payment&state=ACTIVE&page=0&size=1 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshprojects?workspaceIdentifier=bhlm7mpdsv2&paymentIdentifier=test-payment&state=ACTIVE&page=0&size=1' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json'

_embedded

_embedded.meshProjects[]

_links

Get meshProject

Get a single meshProject. A specific project is identified by <workspace identifier>.<project identifier>. Deleted meshProjects can also be requested via this endpoint, but when a project is deleted the identifier is changed and a timestamp is added, so it is not retrievable with its original identifier. You can get this modified identifier via the list endpoint and the deletionState filter.

Table 87. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Example Request
GET /api/meshobjects/meshprojects/bhlm7mpdsv2.test-project-1 HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json
Host: mesh-backend-url

$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshprojects/bhlm7mpdsv2.test-project-1' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X GET \
    -H 'Accept: application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json'

metadata.deletedOn

Put meshProject

Update an existing meshProject or create a new one. This endpoint supports both update and create operations based on whether the project exists.

The endpoint returns different HTTP status codes: - 200 OK - Project already existed and was successfully updated - 201 Created - Project did not exist and was successfully created

Table 92. Request Headers
Name Description

Content-Type

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 93. /api/meshobjects/meshprojects/{fullProjectIdentifier}
Parameter Description

fullProjectIdentifier

The full project identifier is a unique string consisting of the workspace identifier and project identifier separated by '.'.
Request Body

The fields have the same meaning as the response fields. The metadata.name and metadata.ownedByWorkspace must match the values in the path parameter.

{
  "apiVersion" : "v2",
  "kind": "meshProject",
  "spec" : {
    "displayName" : "Updated Test Project 1",
    "tags" : {
      "environment": ["production"],
      "team": ["backend", "frontend"]
    },
    "paymentMethodIdentifier" : "test-payment"
  },
  "metadata" : {
    "name" : "test-project-1",
    "ownedByWorkspace" : "bhlm7mpdsv2"
  }
}
Example Request

Table 94. Request Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of meshProject datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshProject' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Fixed fields that help to identify the meshProject. The name and ownedByWorkspace must match the fullProjectIdentifier in the URL path.

metadata.name

String

The project identifier that must match the project identifier part of the fullProjectIdentifier in the URL path.

metadata.ownedByWorkspace

String

The workspace identifier that must match the workspace identifier part of the fullProjectIdentifier in the URL path.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the project and can be updated.

spec.displayName

String

The display name of the project as it is shown in meshPanel.

spec.tags

Object

Key/Value pairs of tags set on the project. Keep in mind, that values are an array.

spec.paymentMethodIdentifier

String

The payment method of the project.

spec.substitutePaymentMethodIdentifier

String

The substitute payment method of the project.

Delete meshProject

Delete a single meshProject. The project is marked as "Pending Deletion" and the deletion process is started for all tenants. Depending on their Landing Zone setting they are either automatically deleted or require manual confirmation from a platform operator. Tenants first require the full removal of all additional services like Service Instances (OSB) or Building Blocks. If one tenant still has such active services the project deletion will fail.

Table 95. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshproject.v2.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

The full project identifier is a unique string consisting of the workspace identifier and project identifier separated by '.'.

meshProjectUserBinding

A meshProjectUserBinding is an assignment of users to a project with a specified project role. These project roles grant users a specific set of permissions within the cloud platforms used by the project. The actual permissions that the role have within the platform tenant are determined by the policies set by your cloud foundation team.

List meshProjectUserBindings

Provides a paged list of meshProjectUserBindings.

Table 97. Request Headers
Name Description

Accept

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshprojectuserbinding.v3.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.
Table 98. Request Parameters
Parameter Description

workspaceIdentifier

The identifier of the workspace the project with the bindings belongs to.

projectIdentifier

The project identifier of the project that contains the requested bindings.

Post meshProjectUserBinding

Creating a meshProjectUserBinding assigns the users to a project with a specified project role, which grants them the corresponding permissions within the cloud platform. Before users can be assigned to a project, they must first be added to the workspace that owns that project.

Table 102. Request Headers

This endpoint of meshObject API is individually versioned. Use application/vnd.meshcloud.api.meshprojectuserbinding.v3.hal+json for this version of the endpoint.

Update meshProjectUserBindings

An update is currently not possible. To change a user binding, you must first delete the existing binding and then re-create it, for example, with the updated role.

Delete meshProjectUserBinding

Deleting a meshProjectUserBinding removes the assignment of a user from a project and revokes their associated project role. This action effectively withdraws the permissions granted to the user within the cloud platforms linked to the project.

Request Headers

There are no special headers required.

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshprojectbindings/userbindings/user-binding-name HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshprojectbindings/userbindings/user-binding-name' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response

The response is just an empty HTTP 204.

HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
Strict-Transport-Security: max-age=31536000 ; includeSubDomains
X-Frame-Options: DENY

Update meshProjectGroupBinding

An update is currently not possible. You must first delete an existing group binding and then re-create it with for example a changed role.

Delete meshProjectGroupBinding

Deleting a meshProjectGroupBinding removes the assignment of a group from a project and revokes their associated project role. This action effectively withdraws the permissions granted to the group within the cloud platforms linked to the project.

Request Headers

There are no special headers required.

Example Request
DELETE /api/meshobjects/meshprojectbindings/groupbindings/d81b80f9-70ce-4ed8-8e56-457b4c1296cd HTTP/1.1
Authorization: Basic dmFsaWRfdXNlcm5hbWU6dmFsaWRfcGFzc3dvcmQ=
Host: mesh-backend-url
Example Curl Request
$ curl 'https://mesh-backend-url/api/meshobjects/meshprojectbindings/groupbindings/d81b80f9-70ce-4ed8-8e56-457b4c1296cd' -i -u 'valid_username:valid_password' -X DELETE
Example Response

The response is just an empty HTTP 204.

HTTP/1.1 204 No Content
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 0

List meshProjectRoles

Provides a paged list of meshProjectRoles. These are the roles available for assignment to users on projects within meshWorkspaces.

No specific permission is required to read meshProjectRoles – every API Key can list all available meshProjectRoles.

Table 115. meshProjectRole Response Fields
Path Type Description

apiVersion

String

Version of meshProjectRole datatype. Matches the version part provided within the Accept request header.

kind

String

As a common meshObject structure exists, every meshObject has a 'kind'. This is always 'meshProjectRole' for this endpoint.

metadata

Object

Always contains the 'name' to uniquely identify the meshProjectRole.

metadata.name

String

The name to uniquely identify the meshProjectRole.

metadata.tags

Object

Key/Value pairs of tags set on the meshProjectRole. Keep in mind, that values are an array.

metadata.deletedAt

String

Timestamp when the meshProjectRole was marked for deletion. Only present if the role is deleted.

spec

Object

All fields in this section describe the meshProjectRole.

spec.name

String

The display name of the meshProjectRole.

spec.description

String

A detailed description of the meshProjectRole and its permissions.

spec.rank

Number

The rank of the role. Higher values represent greater privileges. Ranks are used to order project roles, with higher-privilege roles appearing above lower-privilege ones.

_links

Object

currently only provides a self link.
Post meshProjectRole

Create a new meshProjectRole.

This endpoint requires administrative privileges to create new project roles that can be assigned to users in projects.

Project roles define the level of access and permissions that users have within projects. They are used to control what actions users can perform on project resources and configurations.

Table 116. Request Headers
